```go

    clusterGroup := []string{"Inner_example"} // []string | Cluster group (slug) (optional)

    clusterGroupIdN := []int32{int32(123)} // []int32 | Cluster group (optional)

    clusterTypeN := []string{"Inner_example"} // []string | Cluster type (slug) (optional)
```
